study mode faculty would guide single or group of students to take up study of an
approved course via self-learning and discussion-oriented contact sessions
this mode can be also
adopted for enabling student to take up study of new course not yet approved by the senate
under supervision of faculty
all formal evaluation components applicable to courses being run
through any one of the above-mentioned modes will be conducted under direct physical
supervision of faculty
all laboratory components of course requiring use of specialized
facility will be conducted through direct contact
the instructors and tutors for all courses to be offered during the semester are allocated by the
head of the department hosting the program
when faculty members of other departments are
also required to participate in teaching particular course the allocation shall be done in
consultation with the head of that department
auditing of courses
student may audit course in addition to the prescribed academic load requirement with the
permission of dean academics on the recommendations of the instructor of the course being
audited and the faculty advisor
under this arrangement the course will be listed in the grade
card of the student
student should have full attendance in each course
unless the student takes leave of absence
for valid reasons the student has to attend every lecture tutorial or lab session
records must be made available to the student after every lecture
even if the student
attendance falls below 75 the student will be allowed to appear for the exams
meeting the attendance criterion of 75 will be required to score at least grade to pass
these students would be awarded grade if their marks are lower than the cut-off for
grade in course
the performance of students in course is evaluated continuously using their interaction in the
classroom and performances in examinations the laboratory work if any and term-papers and
the performance of students in course is evaluated through examinations and on continuous
the senate will decide from time to time on the system of tests and examinations in each
subject in each semester
minor minor and major examinations are mandatory components of the evaluation of
regular 14-week long lecture course
the minor examinations shall be of 60 minutes
duration and the major examination of 120 minutes
fractal courses less than credits
must have at least one examination
the total weightage of the examination component three examinations for 14-week
long course shall be between 40 to 60 of the total weightage of evaluation measure
evaluation policy has to be known from the first day of the class
the continuous evaluation may include but not limited to interaction in the classroom
quizzes assignments tutorials laboratory work term papers and projects
at the end of the semester student is awarded relative letter grade in each course by the
instructor offering the course considering the performance of the student during the semester
with respect to those of the other students registered in the course
it is proposed that ten
regular letter grades namely a- b- c- and shall be awarded in each course
each letter grade is associated with numerical equivalent on 10-point scale shown in table
in addition there are four special letter grades namely and which stand for incomplete
satisfactory thesis continuation and unsatisfactory respectively
the faculty member shall
upload grades on the portal as per stipulated time schedule
grade card and transcript

iit jodhpur grade card and transcript will only indicate the courses
credits and grades completed at iit jodhpur and the total number of credits without grades
earned in other academic institutions in particular semester if applicable

related to admissions to the academic programmes may be waived in special circumstances by

such exceptions have to be reported to the senate

days from the date of the missed examination explaining the reasons for their absence
applications received after this period need not be entertained

make-up examination will be given under exceptional circumstances such as admission to
hospital due to illness

qualifier requirements of ph
the following four components together will constitute qualifier candidacy requirements for
student and for ph
candidate to be eligible for the enhanced srf fellowship
completed course requirements with the minimum cgpa specified in section 12
cleared comprehensive examination
successful presentation on state of the art of the chosen field of research
successful presentation and defense of research proposal
students are normally expected to complete successfully the qualifier requirements
before the beginning of the fifth semester of his her registration in the ph
program and in any
case not later than the beginning of the sixth semester after their registration in the ph
part-time and direct ph
candidates will need to complete qualifier requirements
before the beginning of the seventh semester
candidates will need to complete
qualifier requirements before the beginning of the fifth semester and in any case not later than
the beginning of the sixth semester after their registration in the program
degree students the 16 credits associated with the
project ii are to be converted to the
comprehensive examination of ph
the comprehensive examination must be designed to test the general capability of the
student and the breadth of his her knowledge in the discipline and areas related to the
field of research
the comprehensive examination shall be conducted by comprehensive examination
committee of the department idrp
the comprehensive examination will consist of written test with three papers
departments will offer at least papers for conducting the comprehensive examination
each paper will have broad coverage of one essential sub-area of the department
content of these papers will be approved by the academic committee and senate
syllabus of papers for the comprehensive examination will not be the same as courses
offered by the department
it must be designed to test the breadth of the knowledge in
the src will specify set of three papers as comprehensive requirements for particular
these three papers may be selected from across the departments
the comprehensive examination requirements shall be intimated to the ph
within two weeks of src formation
all comprehensive examinations will be scheduled on two fixed days in year
coincide with the annual progress evaluation day of doctoral candidates
decide to appear for three papers on the same day or on different days
student can appear in the comprehensive examination before he she has completed
the course requirements and satisfied the minimum specified cgpa requirement

assessment of the work of the candidates
annual progress work during the thesis work shall be assessed by the doctoral
committee and report will be submitted to the dean through the supervisor
the doctoral committee will be formed after 1st semester and before end of second
thesis and examination
the thesis will be submitted after an open seminar presented by the candidate and
the approval of the doctoral committee
at least two patents or equivalent ip right document filed is essential for
submitting the thesis
each candidate shall submit four print copies and pdf format of the thesis duly
certified by the supervisor and the co-supervisor for evaluation after completion
of the required period
panel of examiners shall be submitted before the expected date of submission of
the thesis by the supervisor in consultation with the doctoral committee
panel shall include eight examiners who are experts in the field of the study
undertaken by the candidate three of these shall be from abroad
the supervisors may go for the consent of the examiners before proposing the
names in the examiner list
in the thesis evaluation form the points of judgment of the thesis can be the
novelty contribution of the product development translation
after approval of thesis by the external and the internal examiners the viva voce
examination will be held to adjudge the proficiency of the candidate in the
subject allied to the candidate field of work
if the thesis is rejected by more than one examiner it will stand rejected and shall
not be referred to any other examiner
however in the event the thesis is rejected
by only one examiner it will be referred to another examiner from among the
in case the thesis is approved by this examiner it will be
considered as unanimously approved else the respective chairman senate may
advise course of action
if one or more examiner recommends re-submission modification of thesis the
same shall be done within maximum period of six months from the date of
intimation to the candidate
if the report from all the external examiners is not received within three months
copy of thesis will be sent to another examiner from amongst the approved panel
defense will be conducted in the presence of doctoral committee and one of the
external examiners who has examined the thesis

welcome to the civil and infrastructure engineering
the rapidly urbanizing society and increasing quality of life demand reliable and intelligent infrastructure systems which are capable of catering to the societal needs at different scales from an individual to the community level
consequently the civil and infrastructure industry has undergone profound changes and is constantly evolving
however the new-age designs and innovations in the civil and infrastructure industry can only be driven by group of engineering graduates having multidisciplinary training and sound understanding of emerging technologies
the department of civil and infrastructure engineering iit jodhpur esatablished in january 2020
we started academics programs in the academic year 2020-2021
the department offers unique programs that incorporate and integrate the elements of conventional civil engineering with advanced transformative technologies such as artificial intelligence ai cyber-physical-systems cps digital twins dt and automated management and information systems
additionally major thrust is also planned on the design implementation and maintenance of large-scale integrated infrastructure systems across different domains
the focus areas of the department are
energy and environment
building sciences safety and services
applications of ai iot and cps in civil and infrastructure engineering
smart and integrated infrastructure
urban architecture and planning
construction technology and management
water resources engineering
the department strives to be an internationally renowned centre of excellence in education research and innovation with major focus on sustainability and digitalization of infrastructure
develop unique courses in the field of civil and infrastructure engineering through advanced ug and pg programs with multidisciplinary perspective
establish high quality teaching and research facilities in the areas of smart resilient and sustainable infrastructure engineering to foster the needs of society
promote consilient research through application of ai ml cyber-physical-systems digital twin and advanced visualization in the areas of energy environment transportation and construction
promote innovative and entrepreneurial activities through intellectual property generation and transfer
nurture the potential of students to become future leaders in the civil engineering industry for leadership achievements scientific breakthroughs and social welfare

saran aadhar on being elected as the associate of indian academy of sciences
through undergraduate programs the department aims to provide an expanded but holistic understanding of different civil and infrastructure systems and an in-depth understanding of the differences similarities and relations between different scales and components of it
the students will be trained to integrate conventional methods with emerging technologies to design intelligent civil and infrastructure systems from multidisciplinary perspective
they also get exposed to advanced transformative techniques such as internet-of-things iot machine learning big data cyber-physical systems and digital twin dt in the design and maintenance of different civil and infrastructure systems
the undergraduate programs offered by the department are as follows
tech regular civil and infrastrcuture engineering
tech civil and infrastrcuture engineering with specialization in environmental engineering
tech civil and infrastrcuture engineering with specialization in smart infrastructure
in energy infrastructure
the department offers two graduate programs in civil and infrastructure engineering
the program constitutes unique value-added model that allows students to select courses from specialized stream electives and
tech electives buckets to build their knowledge in specialized stream and gain skills they would need to enter into the desired industry
specialized courses are designed to tap rapidly changing energy and environment market while employing emerging technologies
furthermore it builds platform for multidisciplinary research to unravel complex problems associated with the urban environment and global energy infrastructure
the graduate program offered by the department are as follows
tech tech-ph in civil and infrastructure engineering with specialization in energy
to cater to future needs and emerging infrastructure this program exclusively designed with tremendous focus on energy sources such as solar wind and hydropower
the program is offered to the students candidates with diverse engineering backgrounds from india and abroad who are interested in learning and applying the fundamental and advanced technologies energy conversion transmission distribution storage and conservation in different areas of energy engineering
the program equips students with unique set of skills desired in multidisciplinary and dynamic energy industries
tech tech-ph in civil and infrastructure engineering with specialization in environmental engineering
the program aims to produce scientifically and technologically resourceful professionals with broad knowledge of environmental processes and engineering techniques integrated with basic knowledge of biosafety toxicology and other public health issues required in identifying emerging complex problems at the interface of environmental engineering and public health and creatively developing effective solutions
this specially tailored program will enable students to think proactively and preemptively while confronting public health challenges emerging out of local and global environmental issues
the integration of major thrust areas of civil infrastructure and environmental engineering with public health in this cross-disciplinary program will enable graduates to interface between urban development and the sustainable environment

in environmental engineering

programs in all five major domains of civil infrastructure engineering
geotechnical and geological engineering

national highway authority of india nhai signed mou with iitj on friday 24th october 2020
the mou will facilitate the joint working of the two organizations in various domains including transportation engineering structural engineering geotechnical engineering hydraulics engineering infrastructure systems earthquake engineering urban and rural planning and disaster management and planning
this mou will also allow iit jodhpur undergraduate and postgraduate students to undertake paid internships in any of the above-mentioned fields
this collaboration will help to bridge the industry-institution gap and develop technologies which can be adopted in practice
welcome to the department of computer science engineering
computer science and engineering today plays major role in transforming every aspect of human life in addressing social challenges and catalyzing the ongoing wave of the industrial revolution
the department is driven by its commitment to excel in next generation technology development and research
our mission is to strengthen industry-academia collaborations and prepare our students to contribute to multi-disciplinary projects and for solving problems of national interest
to be among the top 10 departments in terms of research contributions practical impact and applications of computer science and engineering in the country in the next years and internationally well known in some focused areas in the next years
some of our missions are to achieve excellence in research in fundamental as well as applied areas of cse and allied subject for innovative discoveries
develop an academic ecosystem by collaborating
and develop and support the notion of computing for all across disciplines at the institute
our missions are to achieve excellence in research in fundamental as well as applied areas of cse and allied subject for innovative discoveries
develop an academic ecosystem by collaborating
and develop and support the notion of computing for all across disciplines at the institute
m1 achieving excellence in research in fundamental as well as applied areas of cse and allied subjects for innovative discoveries
m2 develop an academic ecosystem by collaborating within the institute as well by means of international national and regional institutes
the collaborations may be fostered by research visits collaborative projects joint thesis internship guidance research mentoring etc
m3 develop and support the notion of computing for all across disciplines at the institute
m4 embracing shared dialogue across disciplines and encouraging experiential learning to redefine the contours of traditional computer science teaching and learning
be one of the leading departments in the country for hybrid cse education
m5 define and solve real-world problems in collaboration with industry and develop industry- connect by means of research grants consultancies and collaborative projects
develop start-up ecosystem in emerging areas of computing in collaboration with other departments at iit jodhpur
m6 dissemination of knowledge without physical boundaries
classroom online and other modes of teaching to create workforce which is ready to ethically solve technological challenges of the next generation
m7 provide thought leadership in public policy and ethics of emerging computing technologies towards building an equitable and ethical society

computer science and engineering cse
program in computer science and engineering cse at iit jodhpur aims to equip its students with skills to undertake careers that involve identifying and engineering solutions for real-world problems through innovating upon their core competence in computer science
the curriculum gives due importance to the foundational aspects of computer science as well as aspires to inculcate in students the foresight and expertise to address transdisciplinary technological questions
students can choose from number of elective courses that strive to expand their understanding of emerging concepts and processes across domains such as theory and algorithms hardware systems network and security artificial intelligence machine learning speech vision language and social computing
the program also encourages its students to opt from number of exclusive interdisciplinary specialization tracks that are envisaged to provide coherent and sophisticated understanding of underlying subject-areas to empower them to pursue myriad career paths
some of these specializations are
social and sustainable computing
intelligent communication and networking
the program aspires to produce well prepared motivated workforce who would valiantly embark upon careers in research and industry involving innovation knowledge creation engineering and entrepreneurship
all students who have graduated from the department thus far are currently placed in companies of repute or are pursuing higher education in top-tier universities in the country and the rest of the world
artificial intelligence and data science ai ds
starting 2020 iit jodhpur will be offering unique undergraduate program in artificial intelligence and data science that envisions to equip students with the ability to assess societal health safety legal and cultural issues and most importantly identify their consequent responsibilities as engineers of effective solutions for the same
the curriculum is interdisciplinary at heart straddling computer science mathematics artificial intelligence machine learning data science and their applications across numerous domains
besides artificial intelligence deep learning digital image processing computer vision and video processing the program will be training its students in range of exclusive courses like
data engineering and data visualization
social network analysis
augmented and virtual reality
speech and natural language understanding
the curriculum promises to provide opportunities to its students to explore number of transdisciplinary specialization areas including visual computing socio-digital reality intelligent communications and networking language technologies robotics and aiot
the program will also allow its students to venture into one-of-a-kind management specialization that would focus on ai and technology leading to an mba btech mba dual degree program and scope for entrepreneurial pursuits
computer science and engineering cse
tech program in computer science and engineering cse at iit jodhpur establishes balance between traditional and emerging areas of the discipline by offering students combined knowledge of theory and practice
the program is designed to extend the undergraduate computing skills with up-to-date and in-depth expertise in specialized areas of the computer science discipline
the curriculum is developed in consultation with experts from academia and industry to address the needs of both domains and open wide range of possibilities for students for their future endeavors
students are equipped with relevant concepts algorithms techniques and underpinning principles while developing the ability to solve real-world problems in number of application areas such as computer systems and security distributed computing internet of things artificial intelligence and big data
artificial intelligence ai
in artificial intelligence ai aims to fill the critical needs of the industry and to fill the gap in the availability of highly skilled ai scientists and engineers
the major goal of the two-year
ai the program is to impart rigorous training in strong foundations of artificial intelligence as well as cutting-edge ai tools and techniques and produce graduates who can reinforce the country efforts towards developing ai technologies
dual master with university of albany suny ua
the dual mater program in cse and cybersecurity in collaboration of university at albany suny ualbany
this is unique program that leverages the strengths of the two institutions iit jodhpur in cse and ualbany in cybersecurity
the field of cybersecurity is becoming more critical as we become more technology dependent and there is short supply of cybersecurity professionals in the united states of the order of quarter million jobs
also the field is growing rapidly
students will get an mtech in cse and an ms in cyber security
ualbany is providing 5000 dollar scholarship for our students since we are partner institution
additionally this program is stem certified in the united states which means that students will automatically get 3-year work visa at the end of their one year at ualbany
also currently there are over quarter million open jobs in the cybersecurity
the previous set of students that have gone from iit jodhpur sme we have had 100 placement in the industry or at education institutions for doctoral programs with full assistantships
almost all students have also been able to take assistantships at ualbany making their education even more affordable
dual degree cse
dual degree ai
iit jodhpur has been offering mtech-phd dual-degree programs since july 2019
these programs have been designed particularly for students with an inclination for research
students who have completed their
are eligible to join this program
students complete their
course work and then start their research and earn both
degrees at the end of the program
there are two distinct aspects of these programs first it provides an avenue for students to earn both degrees in far lesser duration compared to if these were done individually and second students are awarded fellowship equivalent to that of jrf from the date of their joining
academically these programs facilitate students to decide upon their area of research by the end of the first semester
after phase of rigorous coursework in the first two years they start working towards the academic requirements of phd that includes comprehensive exam state-of-the-art seminar publications in top conferences and journals and thesis
the students can also work on industry projects and collaborate with faculty from other academic research bodies
this program offers the benefit of phd level scholarship from the first year itself and the integrated courses and research helps in reducing the overall time of completing mtech and phd
the department of cse is currently offering two such programs mtech-phd dual-degree in cse and mtech-phd dual-degree in ai and is continuously looking for motivated and capable students to conduct advanced research in all areas of computer science and ai please visit the research page for more details
the coursework requirements of these programs are similar to the corresponding mtech programs and other support travel support institute mobility grant fellowship schemes in addition to that from the ministry of education etc
and research related academic requirements are similar to the phd program
ai for working professionals
from january 2020 the department of computer science and engineering iit jodhpur has started the executive
in ai program for working professionals
this program runs as combination of synchronous and asynchronous teaching
online lectures are offered on evenings or weekends for the convenience of working professionals
the minimum duration of this mode of
program is years and the credit requirement is the same as the regular
tech in ai program at iit jodhpur
the major goal of this program is to train and enhance the skills of working professionals with strong foundations of artificial intelligence ai and state-of-the-art ai tools and techniques and make them more industry-competent
programs for working professionals
artificial intelligence ai is branch of computer science that aims to create machines to act with higher levels of intelligence and emulate the human capabilities of sense comprehend and act
the core problems of artificial intelligence include programming computers for certain traits such as knowledge reasoning problem-solving perception learning and planning
ai technology development and applications are evolving rapidly with major implications for economies and societies
as the demand for such applications increases there is also an increasing need for building the future workforce for ai
from january 2020 the department of computer science and engineering iit jodhpur has started the executive
in ai program for working professionals
from 2022 this program transcends to its stackable avatar certificate diploma
tech ai in line with the new education policy 2020 for working professionals
this program runs as combination of synchronous and asynchronous teaching
online lectures are offered on evenings or weekends for the convenience of working professionals
the minimum duration of this mode of
program is years and the credit requirement is the same as the regular
tech in ai program at iit jodhpur
the major goal of this program is to train and enhance the skills of working professionals with strong foundations of artificial intelligence ai and state-of-the-art ai tools and techniques and make them more industry-competent
for developing the ai ecosystem this program will be executed in synergy with other
tech programs running in iit jodhpur such as sensors iot cyber-physical systems and advanced manufacturing and design
tech in ai program will offer students with deep knowledge of both fundamental ai technologies as well as application-oriented ai
student completing this program will be capable to undertake careers in industry as well as academia
he she will have the option to explore variety of domains including manufacturing fintech healthcare agriculture food processing education retail customer engagement human and robot interaction intelligent automation smart city aid for differently abled accessibility technology
features of the program
an initiative to cater to the stackable program ideology of the nep2020 for working professionals
easy stackable option opportunities to exit or add-on course to graduate to next stage
classes are conducted on the weekends or in the evening of the weekdays in online mode and students attend in synchronous audio-visual mode
the credit requirement per semester is flexible
students can register for as many courses as they want satisfying the minimum and maximum credit requirements every semester
program elective and open elective courses may be chosen from wide variety of courses offered across the departments and schools including computer science engineering electrical engineering school of aide mathematics mechanical engineering
industry oriented courses such as ml-ops and dl-ops
students can interact and ask questions during the lectures
recorded lectures and teaching materials are made available online
course management and discussions will be enabled via widely-used tools such as google classroom piazza and moodle
there are mandatory two contact weeks in semester
students attend lectures and discussion sessions with instructors participate in offline evaluations and experience the iit environment in person
contact weeks may be organized in remote locations subject to higher demand
students can do their
projects on state-of-the-art research topics across departments
students may participate in projects funded by government funding agencies and industries
expected graduate attributes
after completing this programme student will be able to develop an ability to
comprehend fundamental concepts and hands-on knowledge of the state-of-the-art ai methodologies
design and build real-world ai systems for complex planning decision making and learning solving application-specific problems and to reason about them
conceive design and develop intelligent multi-modal multi-sensory man-machine interfaces
design develop and deploy machine learning based applications using structured and unstructured data
speech text images videos
understand and assess reliability dependability and trust-worthiness of ai-based systems
design and develop ai applications for resource constrained environments
adhere to evolving ethics and privacy laws across various domains and territories
plan and manage technical projects
understand the fundamentals of artificial intelligence machine learning inference engines speech vision natural language understanding robotics and human computer interaction
unify the knowledge of human cognition ai machine learning and data engineering for designing systems
demonstrate hands-on knowledge of state-of-the-art ai tools for real-world problem-solving
ability to develop real-time and robust ai-based systems with specific software hardware and data requirements
build solutions to explore fully immersive computer-generated worlds in vr and overlay computer graphics onto our view of our immediate environment ar along with smart cognitive functionality
demonstrate advanced skills to comprehend and communicate effectively
carry out projects using intelligent cognitive solutions provided by ai algorithms to get more insights in stakeholder management risk modeling intelligent resource scheduling and managing project constraints with intelligent use of data models
program details includes stackable options from 2022 onwards
course structure for certificate diploma and degree program-categories
certificate program requires minimum to credits and 64 hours of contact hours
diploma requires minimum 128 contact hours around 16-18 credits
certificate and diploma as part of the stackable mtech ai program
the certificate and diploma can be obtained as an exit option from mtech ai
the certificate and diploma can also be registered by the student individually
if the student follows the continuation cgpa requirements he she can stack up the credits to earn the next higher degree finally leading to mtech ai as well

are eligible to join this program

program at the department of computer science and engineering cse at iit jodhpur is postgraduate-research-oriented
student works in an area of his her interest under the supervision of faculty member and also has the flexibility to have an industry expert as co-supervisor
the student has to complete the ph
qualifier requirements which involve minimum number of credits by taking courses comprehensive exam state-of-the-art seminar and research proposal defense
the doctoral program salient feature is the independent research work taken by scholars leading to thesis at the end of the program
the average duration of phd
program is between four to five years
the cse department invites students with research bent of mind to apply for admission to the ph
applicant must have high aspiration and willingness to work on socially relevant cutting-edge problems
the department expects that an aspirant has strong foundations in core computer science subjects

jpd with suny buffalo ub
students interested in being admitted into the jpd need to be first selected into the full-time phd program in cse at either institution as per selection procedures of that institution
jpd selection procedures will be initiated within 6-12 months of the student enrolling in the phd program
students selected into the jpd program shall be enrolled on full-time basis at both institutions
before the student matriculates to ub as part of the residency requirement the student must fulfill ub minimum academic admission conditions
ub required minimum score in english for language proficiency requirements
toefl ielts pte cpe cae or det
gate or equivalent as specified by moe govt
of india from india is mandatory
while the program specifically admits exceptional students following their completion of an appropriate bachelor degree it will also admit those who will have completed an appropriate master degree
dissertation will be jointly directed by faculty from both institutions
students will be awarded two separate phd degrees one from each institution
students will need to spend approximately equal time at each institution
when in residence at ub scholarship will cover tuition costs and living allowance stipend
when in residence at iitj scholarship will be at par with phd students at iitj
when enrolled as full-time phd student at ub all broad-based fees will be waived off
covered fees include comprehensive fee academic excellence and success fee student activity fee and international student fee wherever applicable
students will have access to funding for research costs from the laboratory where research is being conducted
mayank vatsa is professor at the indian institute of technology iit jodhpur fellow of ieee and iapr and member of the national academy of ai usa
his research focuses on artificial intelligence with an emphasis on generative ai responsible ai computer vision and biometrics
he is recipient of india prestigious swarnajayanti fellowship and the ieee meritorious service award 2023
he serves as co-editor-in-chief of the ieee transactions on biometrics behavior and identity science journal he led the efforts to establish during his tenure as vice president of the ieee biometrics council
he has also held senior roles at premier conferences like aaai cvpr iccv ijcb and fg
vatsa has contributed in several of india key technology initiatives contributing to uidai aadhaar standards digiyatra the niti aayog responsible ai for all policy national biometric standards and the formation of the technology innovation hub at iit jodhpur
singh is professor in the department of computer science and engineering at the indian institute of technology iit jodhpur
she earned her ph
in computer science from west virginia university usa
she is globally recognized leader in artificial intelligence and machine learning with focus on pattern recognition biometrics medical image analysis and responsible ai
her contributions to the field have been recognized with the highest distinctions including being named fellow of the ieee iapr and indian national academy of engineering inae
she is also an acm distinguished member and member of the national academy of ai usa
prolific researcher prof
singh has authored over 400 publications in top-tier venues which have garnered more than 16 200 citations index 71
her research program has attracted external grants exceeding rs
she holds editorial leadership roles serving as the founding co-editor-in-chief of acm ai letters and the associate editor-in-chief of the prestigious pattern recognition journal
singh work has demonstrated profound real-world impact
her face recognition technology was instrumental in the challenging task of identifying victims of the balasore train accident while her deepfake detection systems were deployed to revent the spread of misinformation india 2024 general elections
her contributions have been honored with numerous awards including the nasscom ai gamechangers award and the facebook award for ethics in ai
she has supervised 14 ph
students to graduation 14 ongoing phds and guided over 200
she has strong record of service to the academic community notably serving as the program committee chair for cvpr 2022 becoming the first researcher from india to hold this position in the conference 40-year history
she regularly serves in leadership roles for premier conferences such as iccv eccv aaai and major biometrics venues
debasis das is currently working as an associate professor in the department of computer science and engineering and associate faculty at the school of artificial intelligence and data science aide as well as coordinator of iot and applications inter-disciplinary research platform idrp at indian institute of technology iit jodhpur rajasthan india
his research interests include vehicular ad-hoc networks vanets blockchain the internet of things iot machine learning ml artificial intelligence ai and quantum technology
das published 170 research papers in top international journals like ieee transactions acm transactions etc and top conferences
das has 23 sponsored projects and consultancy projects to his credit
he has been awarded the early career research ecr award brics young scientist award young researcher award-2024 dst-nsf project award 2025 nstc research project award 2025 from science engineering research board serb department of science technology dst moe nsf and nstc respectively
he has many research collaborations with premier institutions in india and different universities across the globe
he has been engaged in different academic activities inside and outside the institute
he has supervised 10 ph
students and 10 are currently pursuing their theses
he has also supervised more than 50
he is senior member of ieee and vts and professional member of acm
dip sankar banerjee
banerjee is curently working as an associate professor in the department of computer science and engineering of iit jodhpur
his research interests are broadly in the areas of high performance computing big data analytics accelerated computing and computer architectures
previously he was post-doctoral researcher at the network based computing laboratory of the ohio state university where he worked under the mentorship of prof
before that he completed my doctor of philosophy phd from international institute of information technology hyderabad in 2014 where he worked under the guidance of dr
he was part of the center for security theory and algorithmic research cstar laboratory
his phd research was broadly in high performance computing where he worked towards developing novel algorithms and implementations for heterogeneous computing platforms that could utilise multiple multi-core and many-core processors at the same time leading to better performance and higher system efficiency
anand mishra serves as faculty member in the department of computer science and engineering
he leads the vision language and learning group vl2g at iit jodhpur which focuses on problems at the intersection of vision and language
specifically the group is focusing on video understanding efficient vision and language models and multilinguality
anand has made significant contributions to the field through influential resources and systems including the iiit-5k and ocr-vqa datasets as well as indicphotoocr an open-source ocr system for indian language text in natural images

the department is committed towards improving the institute outreach through all phases of technology development
starting from conceptualization down to commercialization and thereby striving towards creation of knowledge in specialized domains
the department mission is to develop strong and sustainable partnerships with research laboratories academic institutions industry and entrepreneurs in order to meet aspirations of the faculty student communities
the department is looking forward to working on problems that throw up intellectual challenges and demand practical and impactful applications and solutions
besides this technology development initiatives and exploration of an idea related to process and design improvement are also of considerable interest
the department seeks partnerships that recognise and capitalize on relative strengths of academia and the industry
to achieve these goals the department is focusing on
development of strong industry collaborations in research and specialized human resource development
identifying and protecting intellectual property
development and and nurturing of international linkages for research and development
the department compute resources include number of powerful servers and workstations designed to handle wide variety of computational tasks including complex data analysis machine learning and high-performance computing
with their advanced hardware and capabilities these resources provide researchers and students to the department with reliable and efficient computing power enabling them to tackle complex problems and push the boundaries of their fields
dgx-2 server nvidia designed the dgx-2 server as high-performance computing system for deep learning applications
it features 16 interconnected gpus that provide high-speed data throughput for massive machine learning and artificial intelligence operations
the dgx-2 is also endowed with nvidia tensor cores which accelerate matrix operations commonly employed in deep learning tasks
one dgx-2 machine with 16 volta 100 gpus and
terabytes of ram is available in the cse lab
it comes equipped with an additional 50 terabytes of storage that is all flash-based
dpu-gpu hpc this architecture combines dpus and gpus in order to accelerate high-performance computing tasks such as deep learning scientific simulations and data analytics
dpus are specialized processors designed for data movement and security tasks whereas gpus are designed for computationally intensive tasks like matrix operations
dpu-gpu hpc systems can accomplish high throughput and low latency by combining the two making them suitable for variety of applications that require large-scale data processing and analysis
the department will have this system shortly
each system will have 128 gb of ram and nvidia a30 gpus
other gpu systems the department has 16 nvidia 1080ti gpu and nvidia a5000 gpu cards for the department users
nvidia geforce gtx 1080 it is graphics card that is often used in deep learning applications due to its powerful cuda cores and high memory bandwidth
it has 3584 cuda cores and 11 gb gddr5x memory with memory bandwidth of 484 gb
nvidia a5000 is based on the latest nvidia ampere architecture and features 192 cuda cores 256 tensor cores 64 rt cores 24gb gddr6 with error-correction code ecc and 384-bit memory interface
general purpose servers the department has several servers that are used for various purposes including web hosting database management and file storage
these servers are equipped with powerful cpus and storage making them suitable for handling large amounts of data and serving multiple users simultaneously
welcome to the department of electrical engineering
the department of electrical engineering primarily focuses on imparting quality education and preparing students to face future technological challenges
the vision of the department is to enhance the research environment and to innovate in pedagogy to address the challenges of socio-economic and human resource development
the department is committed to engage in high-quality research by faculty members and students and in the pursuit of excellence in teaching
the department offers
in electrical engineering with broad range of major and minor specializations and three state-of-the-art
programs in sensors and internet of things siot cyber physical systems cps and intelligent communication systems ics
the department also runs dual degree
programs in intelligent communication systems sensors and internet of things siot and cyber physical systems cps as well as ph

the vision of the department is to develop world class teaching and research atmosphere by excelling in fundamental knowledge and applications of electrical engineering through curricular and co-curricular activities
to accomplish this the department offers an undergraduate program in the broad discipline of electrical engineering with embedded capability-linked specializations for enabling the students to pursue chosen career path
tech program provides the core electrical engineering concepts ranging from circuit analysis and design computing control communication signal processing and power engineering
to equip the students with the essential knowledge and problem solving skills the curriculum provides strong foundations in basic sciences
in addition the engineering design component is integrated throughout the structure motivating and familiarizing students with real-world engineering challenges
additional problem-solving skills and practical experiences are developed through design projects and state-of-the-art laboratory experiments
the structure enables the students to shape their curriculum at various stages
this includes opting for department specialization transition to 5-year
dual degree program an additional minor in relevant areas such as entrepreneurship
salient features of the ug programs
new broad-based curriculum and flexible program structure
balance of theoretical foundations hands-on and experiential learning
emphasis on design-oriented thinking creativity and life-long learning
capability-linked minor interdisciplinary and department-specific specializations
skillset targeted towards emerging technologies like 5g beyond communication industry
smart city technologies
prepares students to compete effectively in world of rapid technological advancements
option to pursue entrepreneurship industry collaboration through engineering innovation
startup ecosystems to translate ideas into business models tinkering lab technology innovation startup center tisc research park
expected graduate attributes
strong understanding of fundamentals of mathematics science and engineering with emphasis on electrical technologies for communication signal processing devices circuits computing systems control engineering and power engineering
ability to apply technical skills to identify formulate and solve complex problems encountered in modern electrical engineering practices
ability to model analyze design and experimentally evaluate electrical components or systems that achieve desired technical specifications subject to certain resource constraints
ability to compete effectively in world of rapid technological advancements and assume leadership roles within academic industrial or entrepreneurial environments in the broad context of electrical engineering
foundations for critical thinking that are needed to broaden their careers in diverse disciplines through minor graduate-level studies and the process of lifelong learning
ability to recognize and practice professional ethics in working environment
ability to acquire new knowledge and apply it as needed
to acquire knowledge of electrical engineering principles along with the required understanding of computing engineering fundamentals mathematics and science
to apply the concepts of mathematics sciences and engineering including computing science necessary to analyze and design complex electrical and electronic circuits and systems containing hardware and software modules
to gain in-depth understanding of concepts of signals devices circuits systems machine learning programming control communications hardware design and related interdisciplinary topics
to create select and apply appropriate techniques resources electrical engineering design and computing tools to solve complex engineering problems with an understanding of the limitations through laboratory exercises and design projects
to perform literature review and patent landscaping for innovative research
to adapt to work in multidisciplinary environment
to understand professional ethics and social responsibilities
to communicate effectively
to engage in independent and life-long learning in the context of technological advancements
to conduct product design or entrepreneurial activities
this program is designed to provide students basic exposure to engineering with focus on the various domains of electrical engineering
these domains have been broadly divided into following areas communication computing systems control engineering devices and circuits signal processing and power engineering
the program aims to connect academics to current emerging technologies and industrial requirements in these domains
the program also encompasses rigorous experimental components along with global standard courses comparable to top most universities
the program is also flexible enough to provide students options to shape the curriculum according to their interest
students having inclined interest in any specific area as specified above can opt for relevant specialization
btech with specialization years
the curriculum offers flexibility to students for pursuing capability-linked specializations of their choice
the department specializations are designed to enable students to lead technological innovations addressing the emerging industrial and societal challenges in various domains of electrical engineering
the ee students can opt for any one of the departmental specializations as mentioned below
the in-depth understanding and technical skills acquired through these specializations will enable graduates to play vital role in advancement of technologies such as 5g 6g communications smart cities smart healthcare and industry
students with research inclination also have options for 5-year

iit jodhpur also provides options to btech students to earn tech-mba degree via transition program
students having inclination towards business can opt for this dual-degree program at the start of 5th semester
this program offers range of specializations such as business analytics cyber security financial engineering technology consulting technology product management
the tech-mba is reflection of the growing demand for business leaders to have an exposure in various technological fields such as artificial intelligence ai fintech and robotics
tech-mba is new wholesome program totally focussing on the tech sector such as digital finance data analytics and ai as well as digital transformation
the aim of such program is to enable students to apply their tech expertise within business context
the program focuses on covering important aspects of corporate strategy analysis of top tech companies like amazon google and tech-centric companies such as start-ups in addition to business strategy
the economics and operations are going to be introduced with strong emphasis on the digital economy and supply chain in e-commerce companies respectively

phd program at department of electrical engineering
the department of electrical engineering offers phd in wide range of emerging and challenging research areas of electrical engineering and allied interdisciplinary areas of communication engineering rf microwaves photonics control engineering power engineering signal processing and computing systems and microelectronics vlsi
the areas can also be mapped with the current technology tracks of the department that include 5g and beyond communication signal processing interpretation cyber-physical systems nano-electronics integrated circuits smart grid embedded systems soc and artificial intelligence internet-of-things iot
please visit research overview to know the associated research areas laboratories and faculty members associated with each technology track and research area
our phd students are trained to conduct high-quality cutting-edge research demonstrated through tangible deliverables and to publish in top ranking journals and conferences
specially-designed courses on technical communication and intellectual property rights enable students in quality expression as well as patent landscaping for potential ip and business translation of their work
weekly colloquium enables the students to keep open avenues of sharing ideas and learning from peers
students have round-the-clock access to high-end research and computational facilities and also have the opportunity of one additional year of fellowship after thesis submission to engage in translational and entrepreneurial initiatives arising out of their phd work
on graduation our doctoral students are trained in critical thinking research development operations and management of emerging technological challenges for both industry and academia

faculty members of the department of electrical engineering are keen to collaborate with individuals from academia laboratories and industry in india and abroad in areas of mutual interest
some of the current collaborations are as follows
collaborations research group at iit jodhpur is developing compact models for spice circuit simulation in collaboration with uc berkeley
collaborations with carleton university joint research on signal integrity and power integrity is going on actively
further one of our faculty members is an adjunct faculty member at carleton university
collaborations with tima laboratory collaboration is on design of high-speed ics and on-chip noise jitter modeling
collaborations this collaboration focuses on cooperative control of passivity-short systems
passivity is defined as an input-output behavior of dynamical system and closely related to the principle of energy conservation
in practice however most of the systems are not well behaved and possess shortage of passivity or non-passiveness in their operation
the scope of this collaboration deals with the analysis and synthesis of the networks comprising the passive-short systems
collaborations with ntnu iit jodhpur is actively involved in research related to mitigating the challenges in physical layer security of communication systems and improving the performance of free space optical communication systems
collaborations this collaboration focuses on macromodeling and eda algorithm development for vlsi systems
phd student is being jointly supervised by faculty members from both the institutes
collaborations this collaboration focuses on secure coordination and control of multi-agent systems
the collaboration is part of the nm-icps technology innovation hub tih in robotics and autonomous systems proposed by iisc bangalore
the scope of collaboration includes designing distributed guidance and control strategies for the multivehicle network systems for their secure and robust coordination and control against malicious adversaries
collaborations there are collaborations among multiple groups of iit jodhpur and iit delhi
these collaborations involve the performance analysis of 5g and beyond communication systems and exploring the ways of improving physical layer security ii data processing and machine learning for the sensors data iii detection of breast cancer through optical techniques iv implementation of mmwave antennas for 5g test bed user equipment
collaborations research group at iit jodhpur is working in collaboration with iit kanpur for the characterization and modeling of advanced semiconductor devices measurement of microwave and mmwave antennas and circuits
collaborations with iit mandi research on high-speed system design and noise modeling in vlsi systems is going on
there is phd student jointly supervised by faculty members from both the institutes
collaborations the collaboration with iiit-mk is on neuromorphic circuits and systems
collaborationscollaborationscollaborationscollaborationscollaborations iitj is collaborating with these institutions for the design and development of an indigenous dual frequency navic receiver
iitj work includes design and development of baseband signal processing algorithms for correlator receivers that perform signal acquisition code and carrier tracking control lock detection accumulated delta range computation and data demodulation
these algorithms would be translated to digital asic based correlator hardware by iit bombay iit madras iist thiruvananthapuram sameer
isro is providing required technological know-how for various aspects related to system engineering for navic receivers

welcome to the department of mathematics
mathematics being the basis of many disciplines is subject that evolves with time and creates new theories to solve real-world challenging problems
our department has been taking leading role in developing new methods to model such situations that can be used in diverse areas of computer science engineering and basic sciences
the department has faculty with research interests in the areas of algebra mathematical physics scientific computation numerical analysis partial differential equations topological dynamics low dimensional chaos dynamical systems renormalization in low-dimensional dynamics wavelet analysis fractional transform theory image processing financial risk analysis categorical data analysis reliability theory applied probability
we are excited to offer high-quality programs at postgraduate level for students who wish to apply math to science or engineering such as two-year
program in mathematics four-year
tech program in mathematics-data and computational sciences two year
tech program in data and computational sciences
we also offer an
dual degree program in data and computational sciences and ph
program with specialization in different areas of mathematics to those who wish to earn deeper understanding of pure and applied mathematics
from the head of the department
welcome to the department of mathematics
the department of mathematics is dedicated to advancing the fields of pure mathematics applied mathematics and statistics
our vision is to emphasize both the fundamental principles of core mathematics and the foundational concepts essential for analyzing key principles applied in cutting-edge technologies
since its establishment the department has been actively engaged in research across various critical areas of mathematics and computing
the department also aimed to explore modern aspects of mathematics coupled with computational capabilities to develop workforce specialized in mathematical aspects of key technologies
with this inclination the department initiated academic programs to address the mathematical needs of both industry and academia
currently we offer various programmes namely two-year
program in mathematics four-year
tech program in mathematics-data and computational sciences two year
tech program in data and computational sciences

minor program in data science
the department of mathematics offers minor program in data science ds from july 2020
the minor program is offered to all the
students of the institute except the students enrolled in
ai de and
the program facilitates the study of multidisciplinary field that makes extensive use of statistics predictive modeling and machine learning without changing its application irrespective of the domain
the main objective of specialization in data science is to equip students with the fundamental concepts approaches and methods in data science
the curriculum includes courses in mathematics machine learning artificial intelligence and their applications in various domains
upon the completion of the minor students will develop critical and logical thinking to solve problems in data science and further will be able to use appropriate technology that aids their problem-solving and data analysis

the semester grade point average sgpa is weighted average
of the grades earned by student in all the courses credited by
her him and reflects her his academic performance in the respective
if the grade points associated with the letter grades earned
by student in courses registered during semester are g1 g2
gn and the corresponding credits c1 c2 cn then the sgpa is given
the cumulative grade point average cgpa indicates the overall
academic performance of student in all the courses registered up to
the latest completed semester
the cgpa is computed in similar
manner as the sgpa considering all the courses in all semesters

the comprehensive examination shall be coordinated by the

these three other faculty members should
have had research experience in the proposed research area of the

else the student shall be given one

this seminar must be given in no case later than the

thesis submission and defense
the student shall submit the thesis within two months of the
prior to submission of the thesis the student
should have preferably at least one paper either published or

the supervisor shall propose list of 10 examiners consisting
of at least four faculty members from abroad and faculty
members from india who have the expertise in the area in
which the student undertook research
for selecting an

the examiners shall have at least years post-ph
no two proposed examiners shall be from the same
the examiners can be faculty members or scientists of

thesis supervisor is not
binding on the chairman senate
in special instances the
chairman senate may identify examiners beyond in the list

from the proposed list of which at least one should be an

in addition the supervisor
shall be the examiner of the thesis
the consent of these
faculty members shall be taken before sending the thesis to
the indian examiners should attend in person the thesis
the examiners shall submit written report on the thesis
within period of two months from the date of receipt of the
if both examiners declare the thesis as acceptable for award of
degree the coordinator academics shall request the
supervisor to hold the thesis defense by the student
if any of the examiners rejects the thesis for the award of the
degree the coordinator academics shall report the matter
to the chairman senate iit jodhpur for further consideration
the chairman senate iit jodhpur will refer the thesis to
third examiner under special circumstances else the
registration of the student shall stand cancelled in the ph
if both examiners reject the thesis for the award of the ph
degree no degree shall be awarded by the institute and the
registration of the student shall stand cancelled in the ph
if an examiner suggests revision of the thesis the student shall
resubmit the thesis after the revision within prescribed time
period specified by the chairman senate under the guidance
of the supervisor
when both examiners recommend the thesis as accepted for
the student to defend the thesis or after the resubmission of
the thesis after incorporating the suggestions corrections
given by the examiners the student shall publicly present the
thesis and defend the contention of the thesis

within india and the three faculty members who participated in the

defense of the ph
on their recommendation

award of ph
degree to the student

one credit for each laboratory or practical class of three hours

papers and projects
schedule of examinations
each course shall have two mid-semester and one end-semester
the mid-semester examinations shall be of 60 minutes
duration and the final examination of 180 minutes
the weightages of
elements of evaluation in different courses are listed in table
no make-up examinations are admissible for any reason
student fails to appear in any examination two mid-semester and
one end semester examinations for genuine reason such as illness
she he may make request to ac for make-up examination within

certificate shall be
furnished from the medical officer of the institute health center
when illness being the reason for absence from the examination
such cases the marks obtained in the other elements of evaluation shall
be prorated for the examination missed
when two examinations are
missed in course the prorating is done for only one examination
marks in the other examination shall be taken as zero

grade point averages
the semester grade point average sgpa is weighted average
of the grades earned by student in all the courses credited by
her him and reflects her his academic performance in the respective
if the grade points associated with the letter grades earned
by student in courses registered during semester are g1 g2
gn and the corresponding credits c1 c2 cn then the sgpa is given
the cumulative grade point average cgpa indicates the overall
academic performance of student in all the courses registered up to
the latest completed semester
the cgpa is computed in similar
manner as the sgpa considering all the courses in all semesters

appeal against termination
student who is terminated from the ph
appeal for reconsideration to the chairman senate
in the appeal the
student is expected to give reasons for poor academic performance
and or why the termination should be reconsidered
the senate shall
take final decision after considering all the available inputs
senate will not entertain any further appeal for review unless
substantial additional information is brought to its notice
application for leave of absence should be addressed to the
chairman ac and submitted with medical certificate if applicable
usually leave must not be availed of without prior approval of the ac
applications for all kinds of leave must be submitted well in advance

from the institute without sanctioned leave will entail loss of financial
assistantship for the period of absence and in extreme circumstances
may also result in the termination from the respective ph
students are entitled for vacation leave up to maximum
of 15 days per semester in addition to public holidays

to maximum of 15 days
for bonafide reasons the student may also
be allowed casual leave for up to days per semester
students may be granted medical leave duly supported

leave shall not entail any loss of financial assistantship
students are entitled for maternity leave duly supported by medical
certificate for maximum of months once during the tenure of their
assistantship or fellowship
male students are also entitled for 15 days
paternity leave once during the tenure of their assistantship or
the leave should be duly supported by medical
special leave is admissible with the recommendation of

present research papers

gaurav bhatnagar is professor in the department of mathematics at indian institute of technology jodhpur since june 2023
he was an associate professor and assistant professor in the same department from september 2013 onward
prior to joining iit jodhpur dr
bhatnagar spent four years as post-doctoral research associate in the department of electrical and computer engineering at university of windsor canada from september 2009 to august 2013
bhatnagar received his phd in interdisciplinary area of applied mathematics and computer science and an msc in applied mathematics from the indian institute of technology roorkee india in 2010 and 2005 respectively
he is also the project director of tih ihub drishti section not-for-profit organisation promoted by and at iit jodhpur established under national mission on interdisciplinary cyber physical systems nm-icps of the government of india
his research interests lie in the broad area of wavelet and fractional transform theory with applications in multimedia security digital watermarking and encryption techniques hashing protocols biometrics image analysis segmentation and completion
bhatnagar is the author of over 80 scholarly publications in peer reviewed technical journals and conference proceedings
he was recently listed under researchers in artificial intelligence image processing in the newly released stanford university listing of the top of researchers globally
he is member of several professional bodies including ieee acm siam and ams
he is associated with several journals as the technical committee member and has been regularly associated with international conferences workshops in various roles such as program chair area chair session chair and tpc member
kirankumar hiremath is an professor of mathematics at iit jodhpur
he is an applied mathematician working in wave-matter interactions mathematical physics scientific computations and applied analysis
his specialization is mathematical optics-photonics and the design of efficient methods to solve real life problems
he did his post-graduation from iit bombay and phd from the university of twente the netherlands
after that he did his post-doc at optoelectronics center university of north carolina at charlotte usa and karlsruhe institute of technology germany
he worked at zuse institute berlin germany
since 2012 he has been with iit jodhpur
he is also member of the interdisciplinary research group on quantum information
his mathematical work on bent waveguides microresonators and coupled mode theory is very well received
puneet sharma is working as an professor in the department of mathematics at indian institute of technology jodhpur
he served as faculty member at department of mathematics iiser bhopal for about six months after which he joined iit jodhpur as an assistant professor at iit jodhpur in 2012
he also served as postdoctoral fellow at school of physical sciences jnu new delhi for more than year
he received his masters and ph
degrees in mathematics from indian institute of technology delhi in 2005 and 2011 respectively
his research interests include topological dynamics symbolic dynamics chaos theory and their applications
among his notable achievements he was awarded first prize for best academic performance in
he also secured all india rank 21 in gate ma 2004 examination
abhishek sarkar is an associate professor of mathematics at iit jodhpur
he earned his ph
from tifr-cam bangalore
he did his postdoc at university of west bohemia pilsen czech republic for more than three year
he served as an assistant professor at bits pilani kk birla goa campus prior to join iit jodhpur as an assistant professor in 2019
his research primarily focuses on nonlinear partial differential equations pdes including elliptic of second and higher orders and nonlocal equations
among notable achievements he was awarded the dst-inspire faculty award dst govt
of india in the year 2018
dilpreet kaur is an associate professor in the department of mathematics at the indian institute of technology iit jodhpur
her academic journey includes phd in mathematics from iiser mohali followed by postdoctoral fellowships at iiser pune under the nbhm and serb national post doctoral fellowships
she was awarded gold medal for securing the first position in her msc mathematics program at panjab university in 2009
she has been serving as faculty member at iit jodhpur since 2019
she has taught wide range of mathematics courses including real analysis number theory abstract algebra linear algebra optimization and specialized subjects like group theory for machine learning and representations of finite groups
she is also teaching regularly in national level schools sponsored by national center of mathematics ncm and indian women and mathematics iwm
she has also organized workshops and academic programs such as the annual foundation school-i 2022 women in maths progress and challenges 2022 and the online sagemath workshop 2021
in research dr
kaur has made significant contributions to algebra particularly in the areas of finite groups conjugacy classes and representations of finite groups quadratic forms quandles and quandle rings
she is the principal investigator pi of project titled computations in wreath product funded by the science and engineering research board serb under the matrics scheme

degree in reliability theory from iiser kolkata

he has been appointed as an associate editor in leading statistical journals namely opsearch communications in statistics-theory and methods communications in statistics-simulations and computations and communications in statistics- case studies and data analysis

welcome to the department of mechanical engineering
the department of mechanical engineering at iit jodhpur is devoted to quality engineering education and pursuits the excellence in research
it is dedicated to preparing students to face the emerging challenges faced by society
the vision of the department is to translate its research and to innovate in pedagogy to enable ignited young minds to find technological solutions for upcoming challenges
the department offers
in mechanical engineering within three major domains of thermofluids design and smart manufacturing
the students also have the opportunity to work with an interdisciplinary specialization in emerging areas such as artificial intelligence ai internet of things iot smart healthcare and cyber-physical systems cps
at iit jodhpur mechanical engineers are educated in way not only to adapt but to define direct change
this is reflected in the portfolio of the current activities of the department
faculty members are involved in wide range of projects in the areas of energy conversion and power systems heat transfer and fluid mechanics mechanics of solid mechanical vibrations robotics autonomous unmanned vehicles design optimization acoustics and noise control control systems rotor dynamics nanomaterials biomechanics bio-inspired thermo-fluids fluid-structure interaction etc
to name few
additionally efforts are being made to introduce advanced concepts like smart manufacturing industry
smart scientific computing techniques high-performance computing applications of artificial intelligence machine learning algorithms sensors and iot as part of solving interdisciplinary problems requiring mechanical engineering know-how
keeping balance between theory and hands-on experience the department intends to provide its students with solid foundation in core as well as emerging areas of mechanical engineering by inspiring critical thinking and nurturing problem-solving skills
the department has active collaborations with aiims jodhpur general electric thermax drdo isro tcs innovation lab tvs motor company to name few
the department has been attracting various sponsored projects from organizations since its inception

reckoned as one of the most versatile engineering disciplines mechanical engineering virtually touches every aspect of modern life from mobile phones and biomedical devices to aircrafts and power plants
it is concerned with technological advancements through the development of products processes and power at scales ranging from nano-scale to large and complex systems
mechanical engineering principles and skills are involved at some stage during the conception design development and manufacture of every human-made object
while design and manufacturing involve the design of mechanisms and the analysis of materials thermo-fluid systems include methods of energy conversions heat transfer and fluid flow
future innovations crucial to the country growth will always have their roots in the world of mass motion forces and energy- the world of mechanical engineers
at iit jodhpur mechanical engineers are therefore trained educated and positioned in way not only to adapt but to define direct change
this is reflected in the portfolio of current activities of the department
our faculty are involved in wide range of projects in the areas of energy conversion and power systems heat transfer and fluid mechanics mechanics of solid mechanical vibrations robotics autonomous unmanned vehicles design optimization acoustics and noise control control systems rotor dynamics micro-nano materials and applications biomechanics bio-inspired thermofluids fluid structure interaction etc
to name few
additionally efforts are being made to introduce advanced concepts like smart manufacturing industry
applications of artificial intelligence ai machine learning algorithms sensors and iot as part of solving mechanical engineering problems
keeping balance between theory and hands-on experience the department intends to provide its students with solid foundation in core as well as emerging areas of mechanical engineering by inspiring critical thinking and nurturing problem-solving skills

arun kumar is an associate professor in the department of mechanical engineering at the indian institute of technology iit jodhpur
his area of expertise lies in high-speed flows and shock waves
he has established the shock waves and high-speed flow laboratory swahs lab at iit jodhpur which focuses on experimental and computational research related to supersonic and hypersonic flow phenomena including fuel injection mixing enhancement and blast wave interactions
the shock waves and high-speed flow laboratory swahs lab is dedicated to advancing the frontiers of research and technology development in the aerospace and defense sectors
in addition to traditional high-speed aerodynamic applications the lab actively explores multidisciplinary extensions of shock wave and high-speed flow research into fields such as refrigeration systems biomedical engineering industrial processing and water purification
ongoing research includes projects on supersonic intakes supersonic air-fuel mixing in scramjet combustors flow control and actuators gas turbine cooling electric propulsion systems shock and blast wave attenuation as well as novel applications like solar ejector refrigeration steam ejector-based water purification and shock wave-assisted biomedical techniques
